## 20 Tips to Help You Win Terraforming Mars (Strategy Guide)

here are 20 quick tips to help you win terraforming masks if you want to there's a much longer version of this on my channel believe it or not this is actually the short version tip number one realize the mines something like this and likewise even if you are playing the greedy engine you can still play some of the stuff in the bottom of the screen other examples of tempo engine cards could be ## My epic TM GIGA Setup feat. Der Maister - TERRAFORMING MARSterclass Ep. 14 part 1

Hello and welcome. Today's video is going to be pretty chill because today we're just going to look at my stuff because I actually dedicated an entire room for terraforming miles. Believe it or not, we got these three pictures. They are of course representing the earth tax, the moon tax, and the jovian tax. The map itself I got printed in some sort of aluminum mix. So, it's one big piece. It doesn't fold. So, it's actually literally impossible to bring to my friends because it's it it doesn't fit in my car. The board is actually so wide that it's even hard to pass cards to each other when you're drafting and stuff. So to counter this problem, we actually invented this genius device that actually enables us to reach everywhere on the map without having to get up from our seat. Yep. So nice attack. And we have some of the expansions. The Pathfinder expansion is my favorite one. This board is already incorporated into the big board, but if you don't have the big board, you're going to use this. Oh, and this one I like a lot. This is basically a dispenser for hand sanitizer. I kind of lost the hand sanitizer part of it, but you know, if you find the hand sanitizer and put it up there, it absolutely works. Then we got some of the user made colonies here. Japetus Leage Station Investor. These are our favorites. I also kind of like Mercury and Titania, but they feel a little bit invalid. Then we have a tag tracker.
